0                                  11859              *
                                   11860              *  SORTLIST - SORT LIST OF ENTRIES
                                   11861              *
                                   11862              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   11863              *    R0 - LIST LENGTH
                                   11864              *    R1 - LIST ADDRESS
                                   11865              *    R2 - SECONDARY LIST ADDRESS
                                   11866              *    R3 - FIRST COL (ZERO IF NONE)
                                   11867              *    R4 - 2ND COL (ZERO IF NONE)
                                   11868              *    R5 - TRANSLATE TABLE ADDRESS
                                   11869              *    R15 - PAD BYTE
                                   11870              *
                                   11871              *  ON EXIT:
                                   11872              *    R1 - SORTED LIST (MAY POINT TO SECONDARY LIST SPACE)
                                   11873              *
                                   11874              *  WE SORT BY MERGING SORTED MINI-LISTS, WE START WITH
                                   11875              *  MINI-LISTS OF ONE ENTRY AND DOUBLE THE MINI-LIST SIZE
                                   11876              *  UNTIL THE WHOLE THING IS SORTED.
                                   11877              *
                                   11878              *  REGISTER USAGE FOR LOOP
                                   11879              *    R14,R15,R0,R1  --- TEMP FOR CLCL, ETC
                                   11880              *    R2,R3 --- PTR,END OF MINI-LIST1
                                   11881              *    R4,R5 --- PRT,END OF MINI-LIST2
                                   11882              *    R6 --- OUTPUT LIST
                                   11883              *
                                   11884              *
 000000                00000 00334 11885              SLWA     RECORD BEGIN
 000000                            11893  1           SLIST1     DS    F

 000010                            11897  1           SLISTEND   DS    F
 000014                            11898  1           SLCOL1     DS    F
 000018                            11899  1           SLCOL2     DS    F
 00001C                            11900  1           SLTRTAB    DS    F
 000020                            11901  1           SLPAD      DS    F
 000024                            11902  1           MLISTSIZ   DS    F                   MINI LIST SIZE (IN BYTES)
 000028 00                         11903  1           SLFLAG     FLAG
 SLFLAG.SLDONE     80 ONES         11907  1                      FLAG  SLDONE              MINI LIST MERGE LOOP FLAG

0                                  12481              *
                                   12482              *  SORTWOPT - SORT WITH FIELD OPTIONS.
                                   12483              *
                                   12484              *  PROCESS WITH COLUMN OPTIONS, TRANSLATE TABLE OPTIONS.
                                   12485              *
                                   12486              *  N.B.
                                   12487              *  THIS ROUTINE IS IDENTICAL TO SORTLIST !!! WITH THE
                                   12488              *  EXCEPTION THAT IT COMPARES WITH COL OPTIONS, TRANSLATE OPTIONS.
                                   12489              *  THE CODE IS KEPT SEPARATE FOR EFFICIENCY REASONS.
                                   12490              *  (IE. THE INNER LOOP IS MUCH SMALLER IN THE NON OPTIONS ROUTINE)

                                   13495              *  SDELETE
                                   13496              *
                                   13497              *  DELETE DUPLICATE RECORDS  (FIELDS !!)
                                   13498              *  THE LIST OF POINTER IS UPDATED.
                                   13499              *
                                   13500              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   13501              *    R0 - COUNT
                                   13502              *    R1 - LIST
                                   13503              *    R3 - FIRST COL (0 IF NONE)
                                   13504              *    R4 - SECOND COL (0 IF NONE)
                                   13505              *    R5 - TRANSLATE TABLE (0 IF NONE)
                                   13506              *    R15 - PAD CHAR
                                   13507              *
                                   13508              *  ON EXIT:
                                   13509              *    R0 - NEW COUNT
                                   13510              *
                                   13511              *  NOTE:
                                   13512              *  THIS CODE IS SIMPLE,,, THE ROUGH PART IS THE COMPARE WHICH
                                   13513              *  DEALS WITH THE COLUMN/TRANSLATE STUFF.  IT IS COPIED FROM
                                   13514              *  THE SORTWOPT (SORT WITH OPTIONS) ROUTINE.
                                   13515              *
                                   13516              *  N.B.
                                   13517              *    IF COLUMNS AND/OR TABLES ARE SPECIFIED, THEY ARE USED
                                   13518              *    TO DETERMINE WHICH RECORD TO DELETE.  IE. WE **DELETE**
                                   13519              *    RECORDS CONTAINING DUPLICATE FIELDS !
                                   13520              *
                                   13521              *

0                                  17670              *
                                   17671              *  CHECK IF
                                   17672              *
                                   17673              *  THIS ROUTINE CHECKS TO SEE IF LINE IS START OF BLOCK.
                                   17674              *  WE CHECK 'IF' AND 'ELSE' COMMANDS
                                   17675              *
                                   17676              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   17677              *    R6 - PFWA
                                   17678              *    CURRENT LINE INFO IS PFLINENO, PFLINE, PFLINEL
                                   17679              *
                                   17680              *  ON EXIT:
                                   17681              *    R15=0 IF BEGIN BLOCK,  R15=NZ IF NOT BEGIN BLOCK
                                   17682              *
                                   17683              *  NOTE:
                                   17684              *  WE READ ALL CONTINUATION LINES.  WE ALSO DIGEST THE
                                   17685              *  LINES (IE. SQUISH, STRIP BLANKS, AND UPPER CASE).
                                   17686              *  NEXT WE BLANK EVERYTHING IN QUOTES AND HACK OFF ANY
                                   17687              *  TRAINLING COMMENT (AFTER ;).   FINALLY WE LOOK FOR
                                   17688              *  A ': BEGIN' OR A 'THEN BEGIN' OR A ':BEGIN'.
                                   17689              *  THIS STRATEGY SHOULD BE GOOD ENOUGH !  (HOPEFULLY)
                                   17690              *
